<div id="review_1164003124" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1164003124" />
    <a title="Mizuki" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16842102-mizuki"><img alt="Mizuki" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1368277474p2/16842102.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1164003124?book_show_action=true">Jan 10, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mizuki" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mizuki" href="/user/show/16842102-mizuki">Mizuki</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16842102-mizuki?shelf=won-t-read-anytime-soon">won-t-read-anytime-soon</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16842102-mizuki?shelf=are-you-kidding-me">are-you-kidding-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16842102-mizuki?shelf=only-when-it-is-for-free">only-when-it-is-for-free</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16842102-mizuki?shelf=young-adult-books">young-adult-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16842102-mizuki?shelf=would-not-read-it-anytime-soon">would-not-read-it-anytime-soon</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1164003124" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17732031696064849351"><u>What you need to know about <b><i>The Young Elites</i></b>, by Maire Lu:</u><br/><br/><b>(1) This is not a story about a grey character, nor a dark character, nor an anti hero, it's a story about a needy, confused, selfish and scared little girl screwing up, using her superhuman power in all the wrong ways, making bad decisions and letting her fear get the better of her.</b><br/><br/>Well... Raffaele or maybe Teren come close to being grey characters, but Adelina, a grey character she is not.<br/><br/><b>(2) Our main characters: The Young Elites (TYE f</b></span>
  <span id="freeText17732031696064849351" style="display:none"><u>What you need to know about <b><i>The Young Elites</i></b>, by Maire Lu:</u><br><br><b>(1) This is not a story about a grey character, nor a dark character, nor an anti hero, it's a story about a needy, confused, selfish and scared little girl screwing up, using her superhuman power in all the wrong ways, making bad decisions and letting her fear get the better of her.</b><br><br>Well... Raffaele or maybe Teren come close to being grey characters, but Adelina, a grey character she is not.<br><br><b>(2) Our main characters: The Young Elites (TYE for short) are rather goofy as a group of rebels.</b><br><br>They don't seem to know much about <b>planning</b>, <b>running a tight operation</b> and <b>public relations</b> when overthrowing the king and seizing the throne are concerned. <br><br>I mean, it isn't a game, it's a dangerous power struggle and lives would be at stake, but most of those Young Elites have been so careless and they suck so much at running their operations.<br><br>I mean, throughout a whole book I didn't see those Young Elites bothering themselves to do anything for PR, they don't do a thing to save the discriminated melfettos, they don't send any message or propaganda to neither the general public nor their foes, they don't address and engage with their followers and supporters in secret meetings(there's one single meeting in the book, but still) ...in fact those Young Elites are simply there and carrying out some mission/stunts (e.g. breaking a prisoner out from the burning stake, killing some Inquisitors and blowing up ships on a festival), and supposedly these are enough for them to gain support from citizens and nobles alike.<br><br>I don't know...the citizens are just expected to cheer for TYE when they assassinate the king and seize power? Can thing really be that simple? I mean, even Al Qaeda and ISIS need to send out messages to their supporters and the general public in some way in order to solidify their support and threaten their foes!<br><br>Not to mention, those Elites also allow a newcomer whom they haven't yet known for sure they can trust to see all six of them in person, they also allow said newcomer to spend time in their major hideout without much checking, also no one is there to keep an eye on said newcomer. *sighs*<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1409721462ra/11013223.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To be fair, there're a few characters who seem to be using their brains: Raffaele, Teren or maybe the queen, but surely not Adelina and Enzo, our MCs.<br><br>However, even Teren doesn't seem to be all that smart when he requests his spy to meet him <i>right at the Inquisition Tower</i>, and said spy also walks right to the front door of the Tower for this 'secret meeting'. LOL<br><br><b>(3) This book reads like a badly written Japanese action and adventure manga--with no depth.</b><br><br>No one is allowed to be bad looking or ordinary looking, all of the Elites are handsome/beautiful or at least attractive looking (there even are Marie Lu's hand drawn artworks to show for those characters' beauty), <b>despite the scars and marking they are supposed to carry. *rolls eyes*</b><br><br>There're a few action scenes which are supposed to look cool and exciting, but there is still no depth in TYE's missions and the story shows no in depth political or social textures of this fictional society.<br><br><b>(4) The heroine is an Angsty Sue.</b><br><br>Definition here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.springhole.net/writing/mary-sue-subtypes.htm#angsty-sue">http://www.springhole.net/writing/mar...</a><br><br>I mean, Adelina really has all the reasons in the world to be bitter and selfish and uncaring! <b>Her suffering is so great so there is a great big dangerous darkness in her!</b> Because her father abused her as a child and said father only loved her younger sister but not her! Poor thing!<br><br>Okay, she makes it sound like everyone else is having everything handed to them on a sliver plate.<br><br>I mean, it must be a cake walk for Raffaele to be raised as a consort and started serving clients sexually since the tender age of 17.<br><br>I mean, it must be an easy breeze for the Spider to nearly die on the battlefield.<br><br>I mean, Adelina's younger sister Violetta is so lucky to be raised by an abusive father who supposed to 'adore' her and she also had to watch Adelina suffered through the years and nearly burnt at the stake.<br><br>I mean, life must be so sweet for the Star Thief to be hated and yelled at for her marking, despite being a noble. <br><br>I mean, it must be no big deal when Enzo <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[being removed from inheriting the throne <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> for being a melfetto.<br><br>I mean, life must be easy for those other melfetto (who are without superhuman power) when they get dragged from their homes, driven out of towns and burnt at the stakes. <br><br><b>(5) The story is filled with justifications that don't work.</b><br><br>In short, being mistreated by a father during childhood cannot cover up all Adelina's bad decisions and terrible actions.<br><br><b>(6) YA romance happens when everyone is on a dangerous mission</b><br><br>To me, the romantic storyline between Adelina and Enzo is annoying and forced, it might be the matter of personal taste, but still. <br><br>I mean, Enzo is no fitting rebel leader when he ignores his trusted advisers' warning and keeps excusing Adelina's behaviors because <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[she reminds him of his dead sweetheart. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Judging from what I can see, I'm damn sure a guy like Enzo wouldn't survive a week in the world of, for example, A Game of Thrones.<br><br><b>(7) The writing is as emotional as a piece of rock</b><br><br>It's nothing new, the <i>Legend</i> trilogy by the same author was written in the exact same bland, emotionless way. However, this problem is doubly annoying in TYE with Maire Lu keeps bothering me, in every single chapter, with all the big talks about the 'lurking horrible darkness' inside Adelina and 'the terrible fear and fury' she is supposedly experiencing.<br><br>To be frank, I can't feel a damn thing.<br><br><b>(8)The only good things I can say about this book are...</b><br><br>(i) Unlike many pointless YA novels, the story of TYE at least is set to go to a certain direction...with the speed of a snail, and how the story is excised is very damn frustrating.<br><br>(ii) The final showdown scene is decently written.<br><br><b>(9) The ending sucks</b><br><br>In the end, after <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[double-crossing the other Elites, screwing up for more than a few times, killing one of the Elites in anger, withdrawing important information from TYE and causing Enzo to get killed, Adelina is finally kicked out of the Young Elites group. And the girl still wondered why those other Elites wouldn't trust her. <br><br>I mean, come on.<br><br>Did I mention that Enzo is killed? No worry, because Marie Lu had already pointed out there are Elites who can revive the dead. <br><br>Yes, Marie Lu spoiled her own plot, she didn't even wait till the second book comes up to reveal it. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <br>Therefore, I'm very shocked to see a highly popular GR reviewer referred this book as <b>William Shakespeare's Mistborn</b>, this book is neither. The plots and the character setting of TYE do look like <i>Mistborn</i>, but Mistborn is a superior book on so many levels.*facepalms*<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385606487i/7184093.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(Link: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://vampirekiki.deviantart.com/art/Uruha-Bitch-Please-204270937">http://vampirekiki.deviantart.com/art...</a>)<br><br>Extra: <i>Updated Reading progress@26/12/2015</i><br><br>Today, 18 pages into the story, I found something in this book which looks REALLY STUPID to me :<br><br>The book's title.<br><br>According to Marie Lu, the most feared and hated plague survivors with fearsome supernatural power are called <b>The Young Elites</b>, the 'elites' as in 'the best of the youths', you know?<br><br>Oh bitch please. Who would call the most feared and hated and supposedly DANGEROUS outcasts in their society <b>The Young Elites</b>? Miss Marie Lu, who are you trying to kid here?<br><br>another reviewer, Paige, pointed out the problem in her <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/819810918" rel="nofollow noopener">review</a>:<br><br><blockquote>
  <br>
  <i>English major problems: you get hung up on stuff like this because Words Mean Things. The villains calling them Young Elites is like everyone in the US government suddenly deciding Al Qaeda and ISIS will now be referred to as Servants of Allah. They sound like far less violent groups, right? EXACTLY.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Now I remember, judging from Lu's previous <i>Legend</i> trilogy and now THIS, I have a feeling that Lu is never an author who has the guts to let her beloved characters suffer and be humiliated for real. So even the 'outcasts' in her stories have to enjoy a glorified title or be viewed as a hero (e.g. Day from Legend).<br><br>I am not amused.<br><br><i>Pre-review:</i><br>Like I'd already mentioned before, Marie Lu is one of those authors whose name is on my blacklist.<br><br>See that? <b>BLACKLISTED, TOTALLY BLACKLISTED.</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421128542i/13326370.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(Link: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://j-rockbrazildownloads.blogspot.hk/2010/09/acid-black-cherry.html">http://j-rockbrazildownloads.blogspot...</a>)<br><br>And judging from the premise, <i>The Young Elites</i> seems like it's <i>Legend</i> all over again. For example:<br><br>(1) Deadly virus/disease plaguing the country? Check.<br><br>(2) A heroine who's supposed to be smart and badass, but this time instead of an American name now she goes by with an Italian-sounding name? Check.<br><br>(3) A bunch of Super Special Teenagers with Super Special Power trying to take down the evil government because they're just oh-so special? Check.<br><br>(4) Of course the heroine, at one point of the story, will join those Super Special Teenagers because she's just that special. I'll bet my good money on that.<br><br>I'm going to keep my distance with this book and its sequels.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="17732031696064849351" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1097477710" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1097477710" />
    <a title="Lauren" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2544584-lauren"><img alt="Lauren" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442501340p2/2544584.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1097477710?book_show_action=true">Nov 04, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lauren" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lauren" href="/user/show/2544584-lauren">Lauren</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1097477710" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13703172154725202875">THE YOUNG ELITES by Marie Lu does something remarkable: take old tropes and archetypes but put fresh, unique spins on them. Reading this made me feel like I was in a world that was already familiar, but then she'd sweep the rug out from underneath me and change things completely! <br/><br/>Adelina Amouterou is a malfetto; meaning, she is marked and ostracized by her community for surviving a virus that made so many others perish before her. She is marked in more ways than one– she lost her eye to the viru</span>
  <span id="freeText13703172154725202875" style="display:none">THE YOUNG ELITES by Marie Lu does something remarkable: take old tropes and archetypes but put fresh, unique spins on them. Reading this made me feel like I was in a world that was already familiar, but then she'd sweep the rug out from underneath me and change things completely! <br /><br />Adelina Amouterou is a malfetto; meaning, she is marked and ostracized by her community for surviving a virus that made so many others perish before her. She is marked in more ways than one– she lost her eye to the virus, and her hair turned shock white. I love that Adelina is a flawed protagonist, not just because she lacks stereotypical beauty, but because she has a darkness inside of her that almost makes her an anti-hero. We want her to succeed even when her motives are questionable, because know society's flagrant disrespect and her father's abuse are what makes her vengeful– and when she learns that she has powers inside of her that can wreak havoc on the world that has spurned her, we find ourselves afraid for her and for the world itself if she succeeds.<br /><br />THE YOUNG ELITES felt both epic in scope (a grand conspiracy, a secret society of warriors, a leader with a hidden secret) but full of specific, almost poetic detail. Marie's background as a designer definitely comes through in her prose. A beautiful book with a totally unexpected ending (that crushed me, thanks Marie!) I know this will be one we'll all be talking about for years to come. </span>
  <a data-text-id="13703172154725202875" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk"><img alt="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597641717p2/66224803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2279068069?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk">Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk?shelf=my-absolute-favorite">my-absolute-favorite</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2279068069" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12738564931774583099"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1517682066ra/24996898.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i> „Some hate us, think us outlaws to hang at the gallows.<br/>Some fear us, think demons to burn at the stake,<br/>Some worship us, think us children of the gods.<br/>But all know us.” </i> <br/><br/>Story ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br/>Did you ever wished that there was a story about a character so filled with darkness, that she easily could be the villain? <br/>Always mistreated, mistrusted and hated Adelina lives a horrible life with her father and sister. <br/>He hates her because she is a malfetto, a survivor of the blood fever left with a marking on</span>
  <span id="freeText12738564931774583099" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1517682066ra/24996898.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> „Some hate us, think us outlaws to hang at the gallows.<br>Some fear us, think demons to burn at the stake,<br>Some worship us, think us children of the gods.<br>But all know us.” </i> <br><br>Story ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>Did you ever wished that there was a story about a character so filled with darkness, that she easily could be the villain? <br>Always mistreated, mistrusted and hated Adelina lives a horrible life with her father and sister. <br>He hates her because she is a malfetto, a survivor of the blood fever left with a marking on her face - the loss of an eye - and silver hair. And malfettos bring bad luck. <br>Day per day she is treated badly and her thoughts are unkind to herself until darkness fills her up. Until one night her father does something horrible and Adelina runs away. <br>Adelina thinks she is alone, but that’s not true. There are others like her, other Malfettos left with markings and powers. <br>They’re called the Young Elite and they’re here to bring chaos and justice.<br>I loved loved loved this story. <br>There was so much action, darkness and affection. <br>There was betrayal and love and fear. <br>I was immediately sucked into the story. <br>It was so interesting and addictive. <br><br>Characters ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>I’m always very much in love with the „bad“ characters in nearly every story. They always turn out to be the most interesting ones. <br>In this story that even applied to our main character Adelina. She was really insecure in the beginning, filled with fear and the feeling of helplessness. <br>But when her powers start to appear and she learns to control them a bit she becomes more confident, strong and badass. <br>The more her character grew, the more I fell in love with her. She was such an interesting and entertaining character. <br>And her look - it was so awesome! Silver hair and just one eyes plus marking? <br>That’s such a really special look. <br>Definitely a nice change to the always perfect main characters in other stories. <br>Next to Adelina there’s Teren who’s probably a crazy masochist with crazy fanatic thoughts. He is so so violent and really really weird. <br>I didn’t like him (even though he’s kind of the villain in the story?), but I felt like he was still created perfectly fitting for the role in this series. <br>Enzo is another main character I liked, but not like I loved Adelina. He was a really silent and serious character, only a few words and conversations escaped him, but he had something appealing about him. <br>He seemed like a lost man trying to fight his way back. I really liked that about him. <br><br>World ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>This book is filled with perfect world building in my opinion. It was filled with a problematic reign and hungry citizens in the streets. <br>It was filled with young people called malfettos being mistreated and killed. <br>And a group of them who wants to fight back, to regain control. <br>The country seemed inspired by Italy a bit, but had also own additions. <br>The thing I love the most about the story was the powers the malfettos gained after their fell ill with the blood fever. <br>There was fire, wind, control over fire, over things and sounds. And there were also illusions, that mixed with the reality so well. <br>There was the darkness in Adelina that fed her powers and made her stronger and more dangerous. <br>All in all I loved the world building in this one and the Epilogue made me want to read the rest of the series immediately. <br><br>Relationships ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>There was a tension between two characters in this story and I felt it from the beginning. <br>In some way it was really predictable, but it was still sweet and lit up the darkness of the whole story a bit. <br>Reading about them made me smile, because finally, finally Adelina got some love, something that wasn’t filled with darkness, fear or hate. Something nice. <br>But there were always Adelina’s insecure thoughts, the whispers of her father in her ear that made her be suspicious and so so sad. <br><br>Writing style ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>I really fell in love with Marie Lus writing with this book. I probably should’ve read the Legend series first, but I kind of wanted to start this one, because I heard the characters are really dark. And I was not disappointed.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12738564931774583099" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Wendy Darling" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2745288-wendy-darling"><img alt="Wendy Darling" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1379959930p2/2745288.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/628302874?book_show_action=true">May 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy Darling" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy Darling" href="/user/show/2745288-wendy-darling">Wendy Darling</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17984141-the-young-elites">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=own-dtb-tbr">own-dtb-tbr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=october">october</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=2014-publication">2014-publication</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=read-2014">read-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=penguin">penguin</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2745288-wendy-darling?shelf=too-many-povs">too-many-povs</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer628302874" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3934441043206027208"><b>3.5 stars</b> Surprisingly dark, with a sister dynamic similar to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15839984.Cruel_Beauty' title='Cruel Beauty by Rosamund Hodge' rel='nofollow noopener'>Cruel Beauty</a>'s and a feel similar to that of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12924275.Masque_of_the_Red_Death__Masque_of_the_Red_Death___1_' title='Masque of the Red Death (Masque of the Red Death, #1) by Bethany Griffin' rel='nofollow noopener'>Masque of the Red Death</a>'s. I admit that the middle lagged a bit for me, I didn't love the multiple POV structure, and there is a LOT of activity going on in Adelina's heart (many references to energy spiking in it, her feelings, etc), but I quite like this world the author has created, and am intrigued to see where the story goes next. <br/><br/>One thing the blurbs don't tell you that you find out i</span>
  <span id="freeText3934441043206027208" style="display:none"><b>3.5 stars</b> Surprisingly dark, with a sister dynamic similar to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15839984.Cruel_Beauty" title="Cruel Beauty by Rosamund Hodge" rel="nofollow noopener">Cruel Beauty</a>'s and a feel similar to that of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12924275.Masque_of_the_Red_Death__Masque_of_the_Red_Death___1_" title="Masque of the Red Death (Masque of the Red Death, #1) by Bethany Griffin" rel="nofollow noopener">Masque of the Red Death</a>'s. I admit that the middle lagged a bit for me, I didn't love the multiple POV structure, and there is a LOT of activity going on in Adelina's heart (many references to energy spiking in it, her feelings, etc), but I quite like this world the author has created, and am intrigued to see where the story goes next. <br /><br />One thing the blurbs don't tell you that you find out in the first chapter: she only has one eye! Which is kind of cool. <br /><br />Fantastic beginning and ending, btw. That ending tips the star rating up. <br /><br />Review to come. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3934441043206027208" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_789660016" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/789660016" />
    <a title="Adam Silvera" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4050629-adam-silvera"><img alt="Adam Silvera" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595433626p2/4050629.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/789660016?book_show_action=true">Dec 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Adam Silvera" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Adam Silvera" href="/user/show/4050629-adam-silvera">Adam Silvera</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4050629-adam-silvera?shelf=signed-copy">signed-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4050629-adam-silvera?shelf=2017-reads">2017-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4050629-adam-silvera?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4050629-adam-silvera?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4050629-adam-silvera?shelf=shelf-awareness-reviews">shelf-awareness-reviews</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer789660016" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6425952293263421035"><b>ORIGINALLY PUBLISHED ON SHELF AWARENESS</b><br/><br/>A Game of Thrones meets X-Men in this 14th-century fantasy from Marie Lu (the Legend trilogy), in a world where "fear is power."<br/><br/>Sixteen-year-old Adelina Amouteru is a malfetto, one whose appearance is "marked" by the blood fever that crippled the country of Kenettra and claimed her mother's life. The blood fever took Adelina's left eye, turned her hair silver, and gave her a power that's remained dormant--until the fateful night her merchant father agrees t</span>
  <span id="freeText6425952293263421035" style="display:none"><b>ORIGINALLY PUBLISHED ON SHELF AWARENESS</b><br /><br />A Game of Thrones meets X-Men in this 14th-century fantasy from Marie Lu (the Legend trilogy), in a world where "fear is power."<br /><br />Sixteen-year-old Adelina Amouteru is a malfetto, one whose appearance is "marked" by the blood fever that crippled the country of Kenettra and claimed her mother's life. The blood fever took Adelina's left eye, turned her hair silver, and gave her a power that's remained dormant--until the fateful night her merchant father agrees to trade her to a suitor in exchange for cleared debts. Adelina runs away from home, and once her father catches up with her, she taps into a great hatred within and conjures forth phantoms that quickly cause his death. It was an accident, but the Inquisitors arrest Adelina and sentence her to burn at the stake--a common punishment for malfettos--for the murder of her father.<br /><br />Master Teren Santoro, the 19-year-old Lead Inquisitor of Kenettra, works to cleanse the world of malfettos with "demon" abilities. When it comes time to burn Adelina in the central market square, Enzo Valenciano, a malfetto known widely as The Reaper, melts her shackles with his burning touch and releases her. He takes her to Estenzia, the northern port capital, where Enzo introduces Adelina to the world of the Dagger Society--a group of Young Elites with dangerous powers--and their mission to find malfettos like themselves before the Inquisition can. Adelina must pass a series of tests before she can undertake bigger missions with the other six Young Elites who can control their talents, and it's here with the Dagger Society that she discovers her ability to conjure illusions is rooted in darkness. But when Teren Santoro takes her younger sister hostage in exchange for information on the identities, location and plans of the Young Elites, Adelina is compelled to betray them, even if it means leaving the undiscovered malfettos all over the world prey to the Inquisitors, and risking her own death as punishment at the hands of the Elites.<br /><br />In Lu's compelling new novel, the characters are morally complex (the Young Elites are not fully innocent, there are depths to Adelina's darkness and layers to the cross Teren bears)--and no one is safe in the book's final conflict. What at first appears to be romance-lite unfolds in tricky and interesting ways. The many twists, cinematic battles and the overriding epic fantasy will keep readers hooked for book two, which teases to be quite the game-changer. Bring it on.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6425952293263421035" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44137919-mikee-readwithmikee"><img alt="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583262285p2/44137919.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1617911063?book_show_action=true">Apr 22, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" href="/user/show/44137919-mikee-readwithmikee">Mikee (ReadWithMikee)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1617911063" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9479014168688931756"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>❝The darkness bows to me, eager for my embrace. I close my eye, open my heart to the feeling, and soak in the delight of vengeance.❞</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>When I first joined Goodreads, The Young Elites was one of the first books I tried to read. But after reading the first 50 pages or so, I DNFed it because I was completely creeped out by Adelina's one eye malfetto flaw. XD Plus, I honestly couldn't get into the story. As The Young Elites became more popular, everyone praised this book and series to no en</span>
  <span id="freeText9479014168688931756" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>❝The darkness bows to me, eager for my embrace. I close my eye, open my heart to the feeling, and soak in the delight of vengeance.❞</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />When I first joined Goodreads, The Young Elites was one of the first books I tried to read. But after reading the first 50 pages or so, I DNFed it because I was completely creeped out by Adelina's one eye malfetto flaw. XD Plus, I honestly couldn't get into the story. As The Young Elites became more popular, everyone praised this book and series to no end. Everyone was excited over The Rose Society and I was indifferent because I never really liked the first book.<br /><br />But after seeing the cover for The Midnight Star, I just knew that I had give this series another try. Now here I am jumping onto The Young Elites bandwagon and praising this book like there's no tomorrow. :P<br /><br />I absolutely loved the concept of The Young Elites and the different powers and abilities that each Elite has. I am so intrigued by Adelina and her thirst for power. I really enjoy peeking into the mind of a much darker character that comes off as a villain. I understand Adelina's anger and her reasons for doing what she has to do. I'm curious as to how this character turns out in the end and whether or not her thirst for vengeance will make her rise to the top or bring about her downfall.<br /><br />Violetta turned out to be my favorite character in this book along with Raffaele! Violetta came off as helpless and cowardly to me in the beginning but after finding out about the truth, my whole opinion of her changed. I really can't wait to see more of her hopefully in the next book. And as for Raffaele, I love everything about him and I'm honestly glad that he's the new leader of the Daggers members.<br /><br />Overall, I'm disappointed in myself for putting this book down too soon because I missed out on such a great storyline of intriguing characters! Now I can't wait to start The Rose Society and see where our characters go. :)</span>
  <a data-text-id="9479014168688931756" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1120679555" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1120679555" />
    <a title="Kainat 《HUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD》" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14717996-kainat-hufflepuff-proud"><img alt="Kainat 《HUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD》" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1517124730p2/14717996.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1120679555?book_show_action=true">Dec 01, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kainat 《HUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD》" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kainat 《HUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD》" href="/user/show/14717996-kainat-hufflepuff-proud">Kainat 《HUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD》</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1120679555" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6488486436206691584"><br/><i>
  <b>"Some hate us, <br/><br/>think us outlaws to hang at the gallows. <br/><br/>Some fear us, <br/><br/>think us demons to burn at the stake. <br/><br/>Some worship us, <br/><br/>think us children of the gods. <br/><br/>But all know us. <br/><br/><u>They call us the Young Elites</u>."</b>
</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1470599537i/19944900.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Teren</b>, man, you got issues.. man,... you need to get your shit together! <br/><b>Adelina</b>, my sweet, sweet Adelina! Only god knows what's gonna happen to you now. <br/><b>Raffaele</b>, dude, how dare you! I expected more from you. <br/><b>Enzo</b>, my baby, Enzo! I guess, i knew it was gonna happen, it's just the way it wen</span>
  <span id="freeText6488486436206691584" style="display:none"><br><i>
  <b>"Some hate us, <br><br>think us outlaws to hang at the gallows. <br><br>Some fear us, <br><br>think us demons to burn at the stake. <br><br>Some worship us, <br><br>think us children of the gods. <br><br>But all know us. <br><br><u>They call us the Young Elites</u>."</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1470599537i/19944900.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Teren</b>, man, you got issues.. man,... you need to get your shit together! <br><b>Adelina</b>, my sweet, sweet Adelina! Only god knows what's gonna happen to you now. <br><b>Raffaele</b>, dude, how dare you! I expected more from you. <br><b>Enzo</b>, my baby, Enzo! I guess, i knew it was gonna happen, it's just the way it went down left me hollow. <br><b>Violetta</b>; yeah, she's got to go! <br>And who is this<b> Maeve</b>? I already like her and her brother! YEAH, LET'S WAKE UP ALL MONSTERS!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1463718471ra/19150307.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>"His chest presses against my shoulder and side; his gloved hand covers mine. A surge of passion cuts through my darkness, and the color of the smoke around us changes from black to red."</b>
</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1463634767ra/19140378.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>^^Shipping them so hard right now! No, no, don't get me wrong, Teren is still my favorite character, that does not mean i ship him with the MC. People often just assume that both are the same, it might be for some readers but not for me. I almost never ship my favorite character with the "the girl". <br><br>Examples.<br>Adrian in VA is my favorite character, but my ship has always been Rose and Dimitri.<br>Dorian; FC. Ship; Calaena/Chaol. (ToG)<br>Warner; FC. Ship; Adam/Juliette. (Shatter Me)<br>Ronan; FC. Ship; Ronan/Adam! (TRC) &lt;-These two are exceptional. SHH.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1463635319i/19140391.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_1071870760" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1071870760" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8429172-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595453256p2/8429172.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1071870760?book_show_action=true">Oct 04, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/8429172-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17984141-the-young-elites">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=ebooks-i-own">ebooks-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=so-happy-i-read-this">so-happy-i-read-this</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=amazing-heroines">amazing-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=re-reading">re-reading</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=until-the-end-of-the-world">until-the-end-of-the-world</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1071870760" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11090253078965185189"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420429845ra/13223235.gif' width='500' height='245' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>It is my turn to use. My turn to hurt.<br/>My turn.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Blurb: <i>Adelina Amouteru is a survivor of the blood fever. A decade ago, the deadly illness swept through her nation. Most of the infected perished, while many of the children who survived were left with strange markings. Adelina’s black hair turned silver, her lashes went pale, and now she has only a jagged scar where her left eye once was. Her cruel father believes she is a malfetto, an abomination, ruining their family’s good name and s</i></span>
  <span id="freeText11090253078965185189" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420429845ra/13223235.gif" width="500" height="245" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>It is my turn to use. My turn to hurt.<br>My turn.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Blurb: <i>Adelina Amouteru is a survivor of the blood fever. A decade ago, the deadly illness swept through her nation. Most of the infected perished, while many of the children who survived were left with strange markings. Adelina’s black hair turned silver, her lashes went pale, and now she has only a jagged scar where her left eye once was. Her cruel father believes she is a malfetto, an abomination, ruining their family’s good name and standing in the way of their fortune. But some of the fever’s survivors are rumored to possess more than just scars—they are believed to have mysterious and powerful gifts, and though their identities remain secret, they have come to be called the Young Elites.</i><br><br><b>Note:</b> I have already read this book back when it came out last year but since the second book’s coming out in a few months, why not, yeah? Plus, I really <u>really</u> loved this story and I didn’t review it properly.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428717420ra/14474271.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To say I love Marie Lu’s writing is nothing but the truth. I adored her Legend trilogy but, I do have to be honest, for me The Young Elites is a whole new level. She’s grown up so much as an author and you can see how her writing is so much better, richer, dynamic and just amazing. The setting is so beautiful and the world is so epic. It’s like Game of Thrones meets Anna Karenina in a deadly Venice. I’m down for that.<br><br>As you already <s>must, truly, lol</s> know, I love me some dark characters. I’m not <i>that</i> into white-soul-honest-to-God good heroes. I like layers, I love complexity and big ass grey areas. I love when authors make me doubt and make me re-evaluate my morals and this book does that. At least for <i>me</i>.<br><br>Like, I can’t tell you how many times, when Adelina was thinking something or plotting and I was like <i>whoa, girl, calm down and think that twice. Gosh, please a bit more gentle.</i> but in the following second I was <i>“wait, no. You go and have your retribution. Make them bleed, make them beg for mercy… make the last pain they’re going to feel the greatest the world’s ever seen.</i> So, that was how my mind worked during the whole book and I loved it. I loved every single second of it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434910658ra/15277402.gif" width="400" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved Adelina and how animalistic she was. Instincts kicked in and she was ready to take down the world. I liked her ambition and her fears and how she struggled to keep the darkness away from her heart.<br>The plot really well built and even though sometimes its development was kind of slow, it was a good kind of slow. You needed to build this… feeling for Adeline and her memories and what was happening to her and her powers and Marie Lu did exactly that.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434910658ra/15277403.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>I just loved how flawed all the characters were. Thank you, Marie Lu.</u>
</b><br><br>The rest of the Young Elites, well, I liked them a lot, too.<br><br>I don’t know if I have a favorite, though. I mean, Raffaele was such a darling and strong character. I enjoyed the beauty he added to the story. Yeah, he’s gorgeous but he also has so much hope and seeing things through his eyes, the energies, the beauty… I liked it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434910658ra/15277404.gif" width="500" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Enzo was a whole different thing. I liked him and respected him as a leader and, even though I liked him as a man and all that jazz, I wasn’t <i>that</i> thrilled about his feelings towards Adelina. I just think she’s the kind of character that is not going to end up with a romantic relationship in the end. It’s a really long way and I do believe she’s gonna be better off alone and ruling and stuff.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418292267ra/12735829.gif" width="500" height="247" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Gemma, Lucent, Michael and Dante also grew up on me. Yes, Dante, too.<br>He was not really a bad guy and, in the end, he was trying, sort of, to do the right thing. Plus, he was needed so yeah, I liked him.<br>Teren was a bit harder to like, I gotta be honest. Not because he was chasing the Elites or being with the bitch queen but because of his self-hatred and self-harm situation but that’s a really personal thing, those scenes made me uncomfortable but yeah… that’s just me.<br><br>The end of the book was the best and, before I forget, I have to tell y’all I do not like Adelina’s sister. I don’t have a solid reason I dislike her, really, I just do. I can’t stand her and I hope she dies eventually. I don’t know if she’s going to help in the future or slow Adelina down or what but I truly don’t care. I strongly feel things can be better without her around. I don’t know.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434910104ra/15277350.gif" width="426" height="205" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>About <i>that</i> specific event <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Enzo’s death <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, I don’t feel like that was the end of it and maybe because of our new awesome characters, <b>Maeve Jacqueline Kelly Corrigan and her court</b> and her powers but I really believe we’re going to see them in action. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Like, I really believe <s>hope</s> she brings Enzo’s back from death. I mean, he’s not going to be the same like what happened with Maeve’s brother but, hell, that’s going to be interesting to see. And, do you imagine dark Enzo and Andelina? Me want. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434910658ra/15277405.gif" width="500" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anyway, I fucking loved this book and if you’re looking for not typical heroes and creepy powers, this is the book for you.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="11090253078965185189" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1865155586" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1865155586" />
    <a title="P " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25327841-p"><img alt="P " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489853536p2/25327841.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1865155586?book_show_action=true">Jan 04, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="P " class="user" itemprop="url" name="P " href="/user/show/25327841-p">P </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25327841-p?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1865155586" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9577120090484278135"><b>
  <blockquote>“Everyone has darkness inside them, however hidden.” </blockquote>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1483625117i/21632249._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>When a story isn't told by a hero who goes save the world at all costs and goodness can't conquer darkness, so the hero falls to his knees and his story doesn't end well. This is what I want to say about my expereince with this shocking Young Elites series. I am being in awe right now for Lu. I can't believe that she wrote such an amazing story like this among many typical YA books out there. She didn't even try to make her story feel good</span>
  <span id="freeText9577120090484278135" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>“Everyone has darkness inside them, however hidden.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1483625117i/21632249._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When a story isn't told by a hero who goes save the world at all costs and goodness can't conquer darkness, so the hero falls to his knees and his story doesn't end well. This is what I want to say about my expereince with this shocking Young Elites series. I am being in awe right now for Lu. I can't believe that she wrote such an amazing story like this among many typical YA books out there. She didn't even try to make her story feel good for everyone. The book itself is unique, dark and wicked. Lu kept pushing me further with her characters and broke my heart beyond repair with the ending. I'm emotinally struck I can't even sit still.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1483625117i/21632250.jpg" width="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1483625117i/21632251.png" width="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I am tired of losing. I am tired of being used, hurt and tossed aside. It is my turn to use. My turn to hurt. My turn.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br>The Young Elites was hard to get into at first; the protagonist, Adelina Amouteru, is not a villain by nature, she's turned into one after her father pushes her too far, it might be hard for many readers to get attached to her character. To be honest, I didn't enjoy some parts of this book because it was cliché and it would have been better if it had been cut out. I went too far in Adelina's mind that I knew her secrets, pain and things she kept inside, yet I felt like everything the author showed us was repeated and sometimes I got bored.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“No one wants you to be yourself. They want you to be the version of yourself that they like.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1483625117ra/21632252.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anyway, I think it's fair to give this book 4 stars, even though it deserves 3.5 stars in my opinion. The ending saves it all, I like the way Lu introduced me to a new character and made me look forward to the next installment. The world I've seen in this book is just the tip of the iceberg, the path Adelina chooses at the end will lead her to somewhere I can't predict, and I'm so lucky that I bought the whole series, otherwise I'll be suffering now.<br><br>Oh I almost forgot to say this, I have one little problem with Adelina, her voice when she narrates the story is flat, I felt no emotions in it at all. I hope it gets better in The Rose Society, right ?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1483517527ra/21619486.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://goo.gl/gzHWfC">https://goo.gl/gzHWfC</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="9577120090484278135" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1696666534" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1696666534" />
    <a title="Ryan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/56788355-ryan"><img alt="Ryan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1468129599p2/56788355.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1696666534?book_show_action=true">Sep 11, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ryan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ryan" href="/user/show/56788355-ryan">Ryan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/56788355-ryan?shelf=august-tbr">august-tbr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/56788355-ryan?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/56788355-ryan?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/56788355-ryan?shelf=library">library</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/56788355-ryan?shelf=lgbt">lgbt</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/56788355-ryan?shelf=feels-trip">feels-trip</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/56788355-ryan?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/56788355-ryan?shelf=need-to-buy-a-copy">need-to-buy-a-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/56788355-ryan?shelf=finished-series">finished-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1696666534" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7920035936303320677"><b><i>"But that's something everyone says and no one means. No one wants you to be yourself. They want you to be the version of yourself</i> that they like<i>."</i></b> <br/><br/>If you go into this book expecting a hero with nothing but good in her heart, <b>put this book down right now,</b> and go read <i>Harry Potter</i>, or something. This is a book about an anti-hero, a villain, a girl who has been stepped on, used, and manipulated. This is a book about people with an un-tamable hunger for power. This is a book about revenge. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472043694ra/20142778.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Suc</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText7920035936303320677" style="display:none"><b><i>"But that's something everyone says and no one means. No one wants you to be yourself. They want you to be the version of yourself</i> that they like<i>."</i></b> <br><br>If you go into this book expecting a hero with nothing but good in her heart, <b>put this book down right now,</b> and go read <i>Harry Potter</i>, or something. This is a book about an anti-hero, a villain, a girl who has been stepped on, used, and manipulated. This is a book about people with an un-tamable hunger for power. This is a book about revenge. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472043694ra/20142778.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <i>"Such power over these little masses. I love it."</i>
</b><br><br>I <u>love</u> anti-heroes. I love villains. Villains sometimes end up being my favourite characters because of how complex and interesting they are. So what did I do when I heard our MC was an anti-hero, written by Marie Lu? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462277149ra/18975161.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"Sorry, always sorry. What in the world can you buy with an apology?"</i>
</b><br><br>If you're sick of "the chosen one" trope, or the main character who's flawless in every way, <b>*cough*</b>you know who I'm talking about<b>*cough*</b>, then give this book a shot. I wasn't disappointed. <br><br>I mean, honestly. If I had to sum <i>The Young Elites</i> up in one gif, it would probably be:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1473901704ra/20528979.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Yes, this book did take me ages to finish, I will admit that. It was slow at times, and I was preparing to give this 3 stars until I got to the ending, and completely <b>lost my shit.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443335672ra/16350504.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"To love is to be afraid. You are frightened, deathly terrified, that something will happen to the ones you love. Think of the possibilities. Does your heart clench with each thought? That, my friend, is love. And love enslaves us all, for you cannot have love without fear."</i>
</b> <br><br>I am convinced that Marie Lu's writing might actually be witchcraft. How can she create such despicable characters who have done such terrible things, and <i>still</i> manage to make me love them? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398233112ra/9388666.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"...I will do everything in my power to destroy all who stand in my way."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1473901573ra/20528951.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now, if you'll excuse me, I'm off to buy a copy of The Rose Society ASAP. <br><br><b><i>"My sorrow turns into anger, then to ice-cold fury. My soul curls in on itself in defense. I am gone. I am truly gone.</i><br><br>I am not sorry<i>."</i></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="7920035936303320677" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
